help 2021-07-02 06:15:58 4: MEMES STAY IN #the-dump
To avoid cluttering up the other text channels, please keep all memes and similar posts to #the-dump. We may make some exceptions if the meme contributes to the conversation at hand in anyway.

5: DO NOT SPAM POST CREATIONS
Please don't post images to #creations or #contest-creations that are:
    ‚Ä¢ Low effort (these include, but are not limited to: youtube tutorials, singular block builds).
    ‚Ä¢ Reference images of a creation that you're building.
    ‚Ä¢ Screenshots of your creation's block count.
    ‚Ä¢ Creations that are not yours.
    ‚Ä¢ Creations that are a WIP. Please post these in #creations-feedback.

Creations posted to #creations or #contest-creations must be of your own creation in Plane Crazy. Please refrain from posting other people's creations or misusing either channel to post images of other things.

6: NO ALT ACCOUNTS
While usage of alternate accounts in the game is completely fine, please refrain from using alt accounts in this Discord server. Usage of alt accounts on this Discord server to circumnavigate punishments will result in a non-negotiable ban.

7: ENGLISH ONLY PLEASE
The majority of the staff team (and the community) primarily speak English. As a result, please refrain from speaking in any other language besides English.

8: APPROPRIATE PROFILES PLEASE
Please refrain from setting your Discord profile's profile picture or status to contain any of the following:
    ‚Ä¢ Any offensive symbol or term.
    ‚Ä¢ NSFW/sexual content.

If we find that your profile contains inappropriate content, you will be removed from the server until the content has been removed.
